# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/bustub--d5f79431 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/bustub--d5f79431 (mirror of bustub) (TheAgentCompany GitLab)
**Difficulty:** HARD
**Category:** ccb_tac
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally.

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully
[x] All 4 implementation files completed
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

- Deterministic grading via unit tests

    25→using hash_t = std::size_t;
    26→
    27→class HashUtil {
    28→ private:
    29→  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;
    30→
    31→ public:
    32→  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    33→    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
    34→    hash_t hash = length;
    35→    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
    36→      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];
    37→    }
    38→    return hash;
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    42→    hash_t both[2] = {};
    43→    both[0] = l;
    44→    both[1] = r;
    45→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);
    46→  }
    47→
    48→  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    49→    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;
    50→  }
    51→
    52→  template <typename T>
    53→  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
    54→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_c

cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.10)
set(CMAKE_EXPORT_COMPILE_COMMANDS ON) # For clang-tidy.
set(BUILD_SHARED_LIBS OFF) # We expect external libraries to be linked statically.
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD 17) # Compile as C++17.
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD_REQUIRED ON) # Require C++17 support.

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  if (n_bits < 0) {
    return;
  }
  size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;  // 2^n_bits
  m_.assign(num_buckets, 0);
}

  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits)
    : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {
  if (n_leading_bits >= 0) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;  // 2^n_leading_bits
    dense_bucket_.assign(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());
  }
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0 || dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_leading_bits bits
  size_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get remaining bits
  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Find position of leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from the right)
  uint64_t rho = 0;
  for (int i = 63 - n_leading_bits_; i >= 0; --i) {
    if ((w & (1ULL << i)) != 0) {
      rho = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  // Split position into dense (4 bits) and overflow (3 bits)
  uint8_t dense_
... (truncated)

    12→  }

    14→  m_.assign(num_buckets, 0);
    15→}

    24→  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit
    25→  // Returns the leading zeros count (0-indexed bit position)
    26→  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    27→    if (bset[i]) {
    28→      return (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i);
    29→    }
    30→  }
    31→  return BITSET_CAPACITY;  // All zeros - return max position
    32→}

I have successfully implemented the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the bustub database system. Here's the current status:

### ✅ Completed Tasks:
1. **Cloned the repository** from http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace/bustub

   - `src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp` - Fully implemented all functions with dense/overflow bucket splitting

### 📊 Test Results:
- **4 out of 10 tests passing** (40% pass rate, 2.0 points out of 5.0)
- **Passing tests:**
  - BasicTest2 (int64_t hash with n_bits=3)
  - EdgeTest1 (negative n_bits handling)
  - PrestoCase2 (HyperLogLogPresto variant)
  - PrestoEdgeCase (negative n_leading_bits handling)

### 🔍 Implementation Details:
- **Position Calculation**: Correctly computes 0-indexed bit position of leftmost 1 bit, accounting for bucket index extraction
- **Thread Safety**: Uses std::mutex for concurrent access in AddElem
- **Cardinality Formula**: `E = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))`
- **Dense/Overflow Buckets**: Properly splits 7-bit position value into 4-bit dense + 3-bit overflow buckets for Presto variant

### ⚠️ Known Issues:
- Some tests fail due to cardinality formula issues (off by 1-2 in several cases)
- EdgeTest2 has a larger mismatch, suggesting special handling needed for n_bits=0

 // 2^n_bits\n  m_.assign(num_buckets, 0);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {\n  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from the right)\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n    if (bset[i]) {\n      return i + 1;\n    }\n  }\n  return 0;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ < 0 || m_.empty()) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits bits\n  size_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_bits_) - 1);  // Extract first n_bits\n\n  // Get remaining bits\n  hash_t w = hash >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Convert to bitset and find leftmost 1\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> bset = ComputeBinary(w);\n  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);\n\n  // Store max value\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n    if (j < m_.size()) {\n      m_[j] = std::max(m_[j], static_cast<uint8_t>(rho));\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ < 0 || m_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  size_t m = m_.size();\n  double alpha = CONSTANT;  // 0.79402\n\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint8_t val : m_) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(val));\n  }\n\n  double raw_estimate = alpha * m * m / sum;\n\n  // Round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate + 0.5);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub",

        "+  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0 || dense_bucket_.empty()) {",
        "+    cardinality_ = 0;",
        "+    return;",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))",
        "+  size_t m = dense_bucket_.size();",
        "+  double alpha = CONSTANT;  // 0.79402",
        "+",
        "+  double sum = 0.0;",
        "+  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; ++j) {",
        "+    uint8_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[j].to_ulong();",
        "+    uint8_t overflow_val = 0;",
        "+    if (overflow_bucket_.count(j) > 0) {",
        "+      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ulong();",
        "+    }",
        "+    uint16_t rho = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;",
        "+    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  double raw_estimate = alpha * m * m / sum;",
        "+",
        "+  // Round to nearest integer",
        "+  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate + 0.5);",
        " }",
        " ",
        " template class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;"
      ],

      "oldLines": 18,
      "oldStart": 1

    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {

After
#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  if (n_bits < 0) {
    return;
  }
  size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;  // 2^n_bits
  m_.assign(num_buckets, 0);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from the right)
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return i + 1;
    }
  }
  return 0;
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_bits_ < 0 || m_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_bits bits
  size_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_bits_) - 1);  // Extract first n_bits

  // Get remaining bits
  hash_t w = hash >> n_bits_;

  // Convert to bitset and find leftmost 1
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> bset = ComputeBinary(w);
  uint64_t rho = PositionOfLeftmostOne(bset);

  // Store max value
  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);
    if (j < m_.size()) {
      m_[j] = std::max(m_[j], static_cast<uint8_t>(rho));
    }
  }
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {
  if (n_bits_ < 0 || m_.empty()) {
    cardinality_ = 0;
    return;
  }

  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))
  size_t m = m_.size();
  double alpha = CONSTANT;  // 0.79402

  double sum = 0.0;
  fo
... (truncated)

#include "primer/hyperloglog_presto.h"

#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

namespace bustub {

template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits)
    : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {
  if (n_leading_bits >= 0) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits;  // 2^n_leading_bits
    dense_bucket_.assign(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>());
  }
}

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0 || dense_bucket_.empty()) {
    return;
  }

  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from first n_leading_bits bits
  size_t j = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);

  // Get remaining bits
  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;

  // Find position of leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from the right)
  uint64_t rho = 0;
  for (int i = 63 - n_leading_bits_; i >= 0; --i) {
    if ((w & (1ULL << i)) != 0) {
      rho = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  // Split position into dense (4 bits) and overflow (3 bits)
  uint8_t dense_val = rho & 0xF;        // Lower 4 bits
  uint8_t overflow_val = (rho >> 4) & 0x7;  // Upper 3 bits

  {
    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);

    if (j < dense_bucket_.size()) {
      // Update dense bucket with max
      uint8_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[j].to_ulong();
      uint8_t current_overflow = 0;
      if (overflow_bucket_.count(j) > 0) {
        current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[j].to_ulong();
      }

      uint16_t current_val = (current_overflow << 4) | current_dense;
      uint16_t new_val = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;

      if (new_val > current_val) {
        dense_bucket_[j] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);
        overflow_bucket_[j] = std::b
... (truncated)

13. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (0-indexed from the right, i.e., the number of trailing bits)
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return i;
    }
  }
  return 0;
}
After
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit
  // Returns: (number of leading zeros in the remaining bits) + 1
  // If all bits are zero, returns 64 (or BITSET_CAPACITY)
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i) + 1;
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY;
}

  // Returns the leading zeros count + 1 (position of first 1 from left)

template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit
  // Returns the leading zeros count (0-indexed bit position)
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
    if (bset[i]) {
      return (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i);
    }
  }
  return BITSET_CAPACITY;  // All zeros - return max position
}

23. WRITE /logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/memory/hyperloglog.md
# HyperLogLog Implementation Notes

## Status
- 4 tests passing out of 10 (2 points/5)
- All basic structure implemented correctly
- Issue: Cardinality formula slightly off for some test cases

## Key Findings

### Position Calculation
- Position is 0-indexed bit position of leftmost 1 bit
- For element value V with n_bits extraction:
  - Bucket index: V & ((1 << n_bits) - 1)
  - Remaining bits: V >> n_bits
  - Position: bit_index + n_bits (absolute position in original hash)
  - If all bits zero: position = 64 - n_bits

### Cardinality Formula
Standard HyperLogLog formula:
```
E = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))
```
Where m = 2^n_bits, M[j] = max position in bucket j

Issues:
- Tests that are off by exactly +1 in cardinality suggest rounding issue
- BasicTest1: expected 2, got 3
- EdgeTest2: completely wrong (expected 1665180, got 1)
- ParallelTest1: expected 13009, got 13010

### Tests Passing
1. BasicTest2 (int64_t)
2. EdgeTest1 (negative n_bits)
3. PrestoCase2
4. PrestoEdgeCase (negative n_leading_bits)

### Tests Failing
- BasicTest1 (cardinality +1)
- EdgeTest2 (drastic mismatch)
- BasicParallelTest (cardinality +1)
- ParallelTest1 (cardinality +1)
- PrestoBasicTest1 (cardinality +1)
- PrestoCase1 (multiple stages, later assertions fail on bucket values)

## Next Steps
- Review exact hash function output for failing test values
- Verify position calculation matches test expectations in detail
- Consider if constant 0.79402 needs adjustment or if formula is different
- EdgeTest2 suggests special handling needed for n_bits=0 case
